***закинуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a> (5618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кинуть.html>ки́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закидывать.html>заки́дывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to hurl <i>(somewhere)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мяч.html>мяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корзина.html>корзи́ну</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баскетбол.html>баскетбо́ле</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> mjač v korzínu (v basketbóle)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the ball into the basket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удочка.html>у́дочку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakínutʹ údočku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put out feelers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:словечко.html>слове́чко</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> slovéčko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put in a word; throw out a hint, suggest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to toss, to throw, to tilt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> nazád gólovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to toss/throw/ tilt back one's head</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закинуть.html>заки́нуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́гу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakínutʹ</b> nógu na nógu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cross one's legs</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закипеть.html>закипе́ть</a> (15347)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кипеть.html>кипе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kipétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***закладывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закладывать.html>закла́дывать</a> (11520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кла́дывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kládyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закладывать.html>закла́дывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakládyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заложить.html>заложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to put, to lay, to place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закладывать.html>закла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:страница.html>страни́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakládyvatʹ</b> stranícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mark a page, to put in a bookmark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закладывать.html>закла́дывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воротник.html>воротни́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakládyvatʹ</b> za vorotník</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put away a lot of booze</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to lay the foundation <i>(of)</i>, to lay</li>
<li>to heap <i>(with)</i>, to pile <i>(with)</i>, to block up <i>(with)</i></li>
<li>to pawn, to pledge, to mortgage</li>
<li>to harness, to put a horse, to get ready a carriage</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to betray, to give up <i>(to police)</i></li></ol>

***заклеить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заклеить.html>закле́ить</a> (14918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клеить.html>кле́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kléitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заклеить.html>закле́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakléitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закле́ивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to glue up, to stick up, to tape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заклеить.html>закле́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakléitʹ</b> oknó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to seal up a window</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заклеить.html>закле́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:щель.html>щели</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakléitʹ</b> ščeli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill/stop up the chinks/cracks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заклеить.html>закле́ить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:конверт.html>конве́рт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakléitʹ</b> konvért</i> ― <span class="e-translation">seal (up) an envelope</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to plaster with</li></ol>

***заклинать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заклинать.html>заклина́ть</a> (17937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заклинать.html>заклина́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaklinátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закля́сть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bewitch, to charm, to cast a spell (over)</li>
<li>to conjure, to adjure, to entreat, to implore</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заклинить.html>закли́нить</a> (18689)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кли́нить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-klínitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-клини́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-klinítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заклинить.html>закли́нить</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заклинить.html>заклини́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaklínitʹ</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaklinítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закли́нивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to jam
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заклинить.html>закли́нило</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dverʹ <b>zaklínilo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the door jammed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wedge</li></ol>

***заключать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a> (8339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaključátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to conclude, to close, to end</li>
<li>to conclude, to infer</li>
<li>to conclude
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključátʹ</b> mir</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>до́говор</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>догово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključátʹ</b> dógovor/dogovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conclude a treaty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključátʹ</b> sdélku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike a bargain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enclose, to put
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključátʹ</b> v skóbki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enclose in brackets</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to confine, to imprison, to incarcerate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьму́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključátʹ</b> v tjurʹmú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put into prison, to imprison, to all, to incarcerate</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***заключаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ться</a> (2569)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaključátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaključátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заключи́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to conclude (with, in), to end (with)</li>
<li>to be concluded, to be signed</li>
<li>to consist (in), to be, to lie (in) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проблема.html>пробле́ма</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v étom <b>zaključájetsja</b> probléma</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">therein lies the problem</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ključ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ение</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally "locking by key"
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaključénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ний</a></b>)

***заключить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a> (2861)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ключи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ključítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaključítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключать.html>заключа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to conclude, to close, to end</li>
<li>to conclude, to infer</li>
<li>to conclude
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мир.html>мир</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključítʹ</b> mir</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make peace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>до́говор</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>догово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključítʹ</b> dógovor/dogovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conclude a treaty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključítʹ</b> sdélku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike a bargain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enclose, to put
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скобка.html>ско́бки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključítʹ</b> v skóbki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enclose in brackets</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to confine, to imprison, to incarcerate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тюрьма.html>тюрьму́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaključítʹ</b> v tjurʹmú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put into prison, to imprison, to all, to incarcerate</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключить.html>заключённый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключение.html>заключе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заключи́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaključátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заковать.html>закова́ть</a> (17238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заковать.html>закова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зако́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shackle</li></ol>

***закодировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закодировать.html>закоди́ровать</a> (24343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kodírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закодировать.html>закоди́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakodírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to code, to encode, to encrypt</li>
<li>to give hypnotic/suggestive treatment <i>(for alcoholism, etc)</i></li></ol>
